# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 23:20:20.008196

### Base Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    freq = [0] * 37
    max_group_size = 0
    max_group_count = 0
    
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        _sum = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        freq[_sum] += 1
        max_group_size = max(max_group_size, freq[_sum])
    
    for count in freq:
        if count == max_group_size:
            max_group_count += 1

    return max_group_count
```

### Input

```json
[62]
```

<details>
<summary>Parser Result: Passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    freq = [0] * 37
    max_group_size = 0
    max_group_count = 0
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        _sum = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        freq[_sum] += 1
        max_group_size = max(max_group_size, freq[_sum])
    for count in freq:
        if count == max_group_size:
            max_group_count += 1
    return max_group_count
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(var_0: int) -> int:
    freq = [0] * 37
    max_group_size = 0
    max_group_count = 0
    for i in range(1, var_0 + 1):
        _sum = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        freq[_sum] += 1
        max_group_size = max(max_group_size, freq[_sum])
    for count in freq:
        if count == max_group_size:
            max_group_count += 1
    return max_group_count
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    freq = 37 * [0]
    max_group_size = 0
    max_group_count = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + n):
        _sum = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        freq[_sum] += 1
        max_group_size = max(max_group_size, freq[_sum])
    for count in freq:
        if count == max_group_size:
            max_group_count += 1
    return max_group_count
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```

```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(var_1: int) -> int:
    freq = 37 * [0]
    max_group_size = 0
    max_group_count = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + var_1):
        _sum = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        freq[_sum] += 1
        max_group_size = max(max_group_size, freq[_sum])
    for count in freq:
        if count == max_group_size:
            max_group_count += 1
    return max_group_count
```
